container resource type ComputeNode {
 resource type CPU {
  property frequency [Hz]
  property load [%]
 }
 resource type RAM {
  using property total
  using property free
 }
 resource type DISK {
  using property total
  using property free
 }
 resource type NETWORK {
  property latency [ms]
  property throughput [kB/s]
 }
}
